══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
_InheritedProviderScope<InMemoryAssessmentHistory?>(value: <not yet loaded>):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this HealthPilotApp Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.

  Make sure that HealthPilotApp is under your MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
MediaQuery(MediaQueryData(size: Size(360.0, 640.0),
devicePixelRatio: 1.0, textScaler: no scaling,

lineHeightScaleFactorOverride: null, letterSpacingOverride: null,
wordSpacingOverride: null, paragraphSpacingOverride: null)):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this
ProfileScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ProfileScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
ChatScreen(dirty, dependencies: [MediaQuery], state:
_ChatScreenState#65cf3):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this ChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GroupChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY FLUTTER TEST FRAMEWORK ╞═════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown running a
test:
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<CommunityProvider>
above this GeneralChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GeneralChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<CommunityProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
Builder(dirty):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this
Builder Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that Builder is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ProfileScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

The following TestFailure was thrown running a test:
Scenario phone-small-dark-1.0x produced FlutterError(s):
══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
ArticleScreen(dirty, dependencies: [InheritedCupertinoTheme,
_InheritedTheme, _LocalizationsScope-[GlobalKey#c5ef3]], state:
_ArticleScreenState#abf9d):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ArticleProvider> above
this ArticleScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ArticleScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ArticleProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY SCHEDULER LIBRARY ╞══════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown during a
scheduler callback:
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this ChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

The following TestFailure was thrown running a test:
Scenario phone-small-dark-1.0x produced FlutterError(s):
══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
GeneralChatScreen(dirty, dependencies: [MediaQuery], state:
_GeneralChatScreenState#a0123):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this GeneralChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GeneralChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

Scenario phone-small-dark-1.3x produced FlutterError(s):
══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
Builder(dirty):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this
Builder Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that Builder is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
MediaQuery(MediaQueryData(size: Size(360.0, 640.0),
devicePixelRatio: 1.0, textScaler: linear (1.3x),
platformBrightness: Brightness.light, padding: EdgeInsets.zero,
viewPadding: EdgeInsets.zero, viewInsets: EdgeInsets.zero,
systemGestureInsets: EdgeInsets.zero, alwaysUse24HourFormat:
false, accessibleNavigation: false, highContrast: false,
onOffSwitchLabels: false, disableAnimations: false, invertColors:
false, boldText: false, navigationMode: traditional,
gestureSettings: DeviceGestureSettings(touchSlop: 18.0),
displayFeatures: [], supportsShowingSystemContextMenu: false,
lineHeightScaleFactorOverride: null, letterSpacingOverride: null,
wordSpacingOverride: null, paragraphSpacingOverride: null)):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this
ProfileScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ProfileScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
ChatScreen(dirty, dependencies: [MediaQuery], state:
_ChatScreenState#c6e32):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this ChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY FLUTTER TEST FRAMEWORK ╞════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The following TestFailure was thrown running a test:
Scenario phone-small-dark-1.3x produced FlutterError(s):
══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
GeneralChatScreen(dirty, dependencies: [MediaQuery], state:
_GeneralChatScreenState#4cada):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this GeneralChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GeneralChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY FLUTTER TEST FRAMEWORK ╞═════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown running a
test:
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<CommunityProvider>
above this GeneralChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GeneralChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<CommunityProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
MediaQuery(MediaQueryData(size: Size(375.0, 667.0),
devicePixelRatio: 1.0, textScaler: linear (1.4x),
platformBrightness: Brightness.light, padding: EdgeInsets.zero,
viewPadding: EdgeInsets.zero, viewInsets: EdgeInsets.zero,

false, accessibleNavigation: false, highContrast: false,
onOffSwitchLabels: false, disableAnimations: false, invertColors:
false, boldText: false, navigationMode: traditional,
gestureSettings: DeviceGestureSettings(touchSlop: 18.0),
displayFeatures: [], supportsShowingSystemContextMenu: false,
lineHeightScaleFactorOverride: null, letterSpacingOverride: null,
wordSpacingOverride: null, paragraphSpacingOverride: null)):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<AuthState> above this
ProfileScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ProfileScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<AuthState>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY WIDGETS LIBRARY ╞════════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown building
ArticleScreen(dirty, dependencies: [InheritedCupertinoTheme,
_InheritedTheme, _LocalizationsScope-[GlobalKey#533d3]], state:
_ArticleScreenState#af27c):
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ArticleProvider> above
this ArticleScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ArticleScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ArticleProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY SCHEDULER LIBRARY ╞══════════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown during a
scheduler callback:
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<ChatProvider> above
this ChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that ChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<ChatProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.


══╡ EXCEPTION CAUGHT BY FLUTTER TEST FRAMEWORK ╞═════════════════
The following ProviderNotFoundException was thrown running a
test:
Error: Could not find the correct Provider<CommunityProvider>
above this GeneralChatScreen Widget

This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not
include the provider
of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:

- You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a
hot-reload.
  To fix, perform a hot-restart.

- The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.

  Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a
route, then
  other routes will not be able to access that provider.

- You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider
you are trying to read.

  Make sure that GeneralChatScreen is under your
MultiProvider/Provider<CommunityProvider>.
  This usually happens when you are creating a provider and
trying to read it immediately.

  For example, instead of:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is
associated
      // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
      child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
    );
  }
  ```

  consider using `builder` like so:

  ```
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Provider<Example>(
      create: (_) => Example(),
      // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has
access to the provider
      builder: (context, child) {
        // No longer throws
        return Text(context.watch<Example>().toString());
      }
    );
  }
  ```

If none of these solutions work, consider asking for help on
StackOverflow:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/flutter
